The `public contributions` by users in Taiwan on `2021/8/30 10:29 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Taiwan` and cities `Taipei` `Kaohsiung` `Tainan` `Taichung `.

There are `137 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/gayanvoice/top-github-users).

There are `1000 users`  in Taiwan. You need at least `35 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
